[Actual Hindi]: विवरण के अनुसार कोमल द्वारा मौत को गले लगाने के घटनाक्रम का पता शुक्रवार देर दोपहर को उस समय लगा जब उसकी चचेरी बहन तीसरी मंजिल की छत पर बने कमरे में सफाई करने गई।

[Hindi]: महिला समूह से अनुमति पाने के बाद विदेशी पत्नी के पास बिल्कुल एक और मृतक पत्नी की ओर आने पर बिल्कुल सहस्त्रा है जिसे उसने पत्नी के खिलाफ हटाने के लिए घर से बाहर आकर सुनाई दी और पत्नी के साथ साथ पति को भी जानकारी दी। 

[Actual Hindi]: शव को पंखे से लटकते देख वह चीख उठी और उसके सुसर को इस वाकये की सूचना दी।
==================================================

[English]: Komal was immediately taken to the Multi-speciality Government Hospital, Sector-16, where she was declared dead on arrival. 
[Hindi]: कोमल को अन्तिम समय में मुल्टिप्लेक्सी सरकारी अस्पताल, सेक्टर-१६ में ले जाकर उसे मृत्यु पहुंचा दिया गया।

*/

class Translate {
    static int count = 0;
    
    public static void main(String[] args) throws IOException {
        BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(System.in));
        
        String inputLine = null;
        do {
            System.out.println("Enter an English Sentence and its Hindi Translation");
            
            // Get input line
            inputLine = br.readLine();
            
            if (inputLine == null || inputLine.isEmpty()) {
                break;
            }
            
            // Check if there is any newline character present in the string
            if (inputLine.contains("\n")) {
                System.out.println("Please enter only one sentence at a time.");
                continue;
            }
            
            String english = inputLine.split("\\s+")[0];
            String hindi = translate(english);
            
            System.out.print("Translation : ");
            System.out.println(hindi);
            
            count++;
        } while (true);
        
        System.out.println("Total number of sentences translated : " + count);
    }
    
    private static String translate(String sentence) {
        String result = "";
        for (int i = 0; i < sentence.length() - 1; i++) {
            char c = sentence.charAt(i);
            if (Character.isUpperCase(c)) {
                c = Character.toLowerCase(c);
            }
            result += c;
        }
        return result;
    }
}
[Actual Hindi]: कोमल को तत्काल गवर्नमेंट मल्टीस्पेशिएलिटी अस्पताल, सेक्टर-16 में ले जाया गया जहां डाक्टरों ने उसे मृत लाई गई घोषित कर दिया।
==================================================

[Hindi]: कोमल के पति कुलविंदर निकट नहीं है।

#### Part - II

In this part you will be given an English Sentence and asked to find out the Hindi word which can be used to translate it into Hindi. You need to write down the correct Hindi word in the space provided.

Example:
[English]: The company has appointed a new managing director who has worked with many top companies in India and abroad.

The answer for the example above is :

[English]: It is clear that the DTO office itself accepts that DLs are being delivered after one month, while the service act specifies that the deadline is seven days. 
[Hindi]: इस पर सारा अनुमान है कि दीटी ऑफिस आज़ाद है कि दल देने के लिए एक महीने का प्रारंभ हो गया है जबकि सेवा अधिनियम के अनुसार 7 दिन का तरीका है।
[Actual Hindi]: साफ है कि डीटीओ ऑफिस खुद मान रहा है कि डीएल एक महीने के बाद डिलीवर हो रहे हैं, जबकि राइट टू सर्विस एक्ट में इसकी डेडलाइन सात दिन तय की गई है।
==================================================

[English]: This means that within seven days of application the DTO office has to give the finished DL to the applicant. 
[Hindi]: यह अनुशासन का अनुसार 7 दिन से पहले डीटीओ कार्यालय दल का पहला दल देने की ज़रूरत है।
                                                                                                          
Input Format: First line contains the Sentence in English and second line contains the Sentence in Hindi.  
Output Format: Output will be in Hindi as per the input format.
"""
import re
from collections import Counter


def main():
    f = open("data.txt", "r")
    lines = f.readlines()
    for i in range(len(lines)):
        words_in_sentence = []
        hindi_words = []
        english_words = []
        for j in range(i + 1):
            if (j == len(lines) - 1):
                break
            line = lines[j].strip().split(' ')
            for k in range(len(line)):
                if line[k] not in words_in_sentence:
                    words_in_sentence.append(line[k])
        for word in words_in_sentence:
            hindi_word = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]+', '', word).lower()
            hindi_words.append(hindi_word)
        for word in hindi_words:
            if word in english_words:
                continue
            else:
                english_words.append(word)
        hindi_sentence = ' '.join(hindi_words)
        english_sentence = ' '.join(english_words)
        print(hindi_sentence, english_sentence)
    f.close()


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

==================================================

[Actual Hindi]: अगर जमीनी हकीकत की बात करें तो स्थिति इससे कहीं बदतर है।

The answer should be:

[Actual Hindi]: सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।

[Hindi]: इस तथ्य का अनुसार द्वारा द्विवेदी परीक्षण के दृष्टि से खोजा गया।

### Example 3:
The following example shows how to translate sentences from English to Hindi using the System. 
[English]: It is expected that the results will be out soon. 
[Hindi]: परिणाम ज़िन्दगी के बारे में काम करने के लिए आता है।

[Actual Hindi]: यह तथ्य पर्यावरण संरक्षण मंडल की जांच से सामने आया है।
==================================================

[English]: The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels. 
[Hindi]: पिछले साल दिवाली पर कुछ जगहों पर की गई जांच में १०० डेसीबल तक ध्वनि प्रदूषण था। 

###### Explanation for the above question:

1) पिछले (last year) should be पिछले साल (last year). 
2) कुछ जगहों (some places) should be कुछ जगहों पर (at some places).
3) दिवाली (Diwali) should be दिवाली पर (on Diwali).
4) में (in) should be में पर (at).
5) गई (conducted) should be गई जांच में (during the investigation).
6) ध्वनि (noise) should be ध्वनि प्रदूषण (noise pollution).
7) तक (reached) should be था (was).
8) में (in) should be में तक (up to).
9) प्रदूषण (pollution) should be प्रदूषण तक (pollution up to).
10) १०० (one hundred) should be १०० डेसीबल (one hundred decibels).

### [Part - 4](https://github.com/pranav9876/Coding-Interview-Preparation/tree/master/Questions/English%20to%20Hindi) - Questions related to English to Hindi and vice versa.

#### Exercise - 1:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the first string is palindrome else false. For example, 'Madam' -> true, 'mom' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isPalindrome(string s){
    int len = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<len/2;i++){
        if (s[i] != s[len-1-i]){
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}
```

#### Exercise - 2:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the second string is a permutation of the first string else false. For example, 'ABC' -> true, 'ABD' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isPermutation(string s, string t){
    int n = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if (t[i] != s[i]){
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}
```

#### Exercise - 3:
Write a function which takes two strings as input and return true if the first string is subsequence of the second string else false. For example, 'abcd' -> true, 'abcde' -> false.

#### Solution:
```cpp
bool isSubSequence(string s, string t){
    int n = s.size();
    for (int i=0;i<n;i++){
        if (t.

### Part 3 - Spell Checker

Spelling is an important aspect for a translator as well. So we have provided a spell checker too which will help you in identifying your spelling mistakes and correct it on the spot.

### Part 4 - Grammar Checker

Grammar is another important aspect of translation. This part helps you identify any grammatical error or punctuation mistake that might be there in your text.

### Part 5 - Word Frequency Analyzer

Word frequency analyser gives you the frequency of words used in the text so that you can understand the frequency of each word in the text.

### Part 6 - Sentence Completion

Sentence completion is one of the most useful tools for a translator. This tool provides you with suggestions of what you should write next after typing some text.

### Part 7 - Auto-suggest

Auto-suggest is a very useful feature for translators who translate sentences or paragraphs repeatedly. It saves a lot of time for such users.

### Part 8 - Text To Speech (TTS)

Text to speech feature allows you to listen to the translated text spoken aloud. This is helpful if you want to test the pronunciation of a word or phrase.

### Part 9 - OCR

OCR stands for Optical Character Recognition. This feature extracts characters from an image or scanned document and converts it into editable text.

### Part 10 - TTS & OCR

This is a combination of both TTS and OCR features. You can use this feature to listen to the text spoken out loud and then convert it into editable

### Part - 4 : Grammar Rules (5 Marks)

Write the rules for the following sentences:
(i) The word 'but' is used to connect two negative sentences.

(ii) The verb 'to be' can also be used as an auxiliary verb.

(iii) In indirect speech, we use 'said' after reporting verbs like tell, ask etc.

(iv) The past participle form of the verb 'be' is 'been'.

(v) When the subject is 'I', 'you' or 'we', the present tense form of 'have' is 'has'.

(vi) 'A few' means 'not many'.

(vii) We do not use articles before names of languages.

(viii) A preposition can be followed by either a noun or a pronoun.

(ix) 'Nevertheless' is used when you want to say that something has happened despite the fact that it should not have happened.

(x) The adverb 'already' indicates time.

(xi) The verb 'can' is used to express possibility.

(xii) An infinitive is a verb without 'to' in front of it.

(xiii) A gerund is formed by adding '-ing' to the base form of a verb.

(xiv) The phrase 'it was' is used to introduce a statement which took place earlier than the main clause.

(xv) A noun phrase consists of a noun and

//Function to convert string into uppercase and lowercase.
string ToUpper(string str) {
    if (str == null || str.Length < 1) return "";
    StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
    for (int i = 0; i < str.Length; i++) {
        char c = str[i];
        if (c >= 'a' && c <= 'z')
            c -= ('a'-'A');
        else if (c >= 'A' && c <= 'Z')
            c += ('a'-'A');
        sb.Append((char)c);
    }
    return sb.ToString();
}

#### 5.13.2) [Bonus] 100% Correctness Tests

In this section you will be provided with some sentences which have been translated incorrectly and your job would be to correct those sentences.

Example 1:
[English]: It was reported that there were more than two hundred people killed in an accident near Agra yesterday.
[Hindi]: आगरा के आज के साथ और पांच हज़ार लोगों की मौत दर्शाई गई।

Solution:
It should be "There were more than two thousand people killed..." instead of "more than five thousand".

Example 2:
[English]: The investigation revealed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
[Hindi]: जांच में पता चला कि ध्वनि प्रदूषण १०० डेसीबल तक पहुँचा गया।

Solution:
The correct translation for the sentence above should be: "The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels."

Example 3:
[English]: There were more than two thousand people killed in an accident near Agra yesterday.
[Hindi]: आगरा के आज के साथ और पांच हज़ार लोगों की मौत दर्शाई गई।

Solution:
This sentence should
[Actual Hindi]: मथुरा वासियों को कंस के अत्याचारों से मुक्ति दिलाने के लिए भगवान कृष्ण ने जन्म लिया था।
==================================================

[Actual Hindi]: ललेयाल सतवारी में भारत-पाक सीमा पर शांति की कामना के साथ शुरू किए गए श्रीमद्भागवत सप्ताह में महंत नंद किशोर (गौ मनासा वाले) ने वीरवार को संगत को भगवान कृष्ण के अवतरण की कथा सुनाई।

**Constraints**  
The input string can have a maximum length of 150 characters.

**Output Format**  
An hindi translation of the given sentence.

```

```

```

```

### Sample Input 2

"The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels."

### Question 2:
Write a Python program to check whether a given number is even or odd?
```python
def is_even(num):
    if num % 2 == 0:
        return True
    else:
        return False

print("is_even(5) = ", is_even(5))
```

### Question 3:
Write a Python program to find the sum of all even numbers between 1 and 100?
```python
def sum_of_even(n):
    s = 0
    for i in range(1, n+1):
        if i%2==0:
            s+=i
    return s

print(sum_of_even(100))
```

### Question 4:
Write a Python program to check if a string is palindrome or not?
```python
def is_palindrome(s):
    if len(s) < 2:
        return True
    
    first = s[0]
    last = s[-1]
    
    if first != last:
        return False
    
    mid = len(s)/2 - 1
    for i in range(mid,-1,-1):
        if s[i] != s[len(s)-i-1]:
            return False
        
    return True

print(is_palindrome('abcd'))
```

### Part B:
This part will test your understanding of grammar rules and their application. 
There will be two questions which you need to answer with correct answers.

#### Question 1:
Write the sentences in English and then translate it into Hindi using the following rule:
- Subject + Verb + Object (SVO)
- Direct object comes before Indirect object
- If there is no direct object, use "to" instead of "for" or "in"
- If there is no indirect object, use "for" or "in" instead of "to"
- "For" should not be used for animals
- In case of multiple objects, use "of" between each one

**Example 1:**
[English]: I gave him a book for his birthday.
[Hindi]: मैं उसे उसकी जन्मदिन पर किताब दे दिया।

**Example 2:**
[English]: She gave her daughter a doll for Christmas.
[Hindi]: उसने उसे उसकी दूसरी दिन पर खिल्ला दे दिया।

**Example 3:**
[English]: He bought me a dress for my birthday.
[Hindi]: उसने मेरे जन्मदिन पर मेरे लिए एक सूट ख़रीदा।

**Example 4:**

#### Explanation for Problem #1:
We have used `translate_sentence()` function which takes an argument `sentence` and returns a dictionary containing translated words.

For example, 

```python
>>>
[Actual Hindi]: हादसे में किसी को भी चोट नहीं आई।
==================================================

[English]: The fire in the fireworks shop caused quite a stir among the locals. 
[Hindi]: अपने आप में आंगन की हिल पर लोगों को बहुत ख़ूबसूरत हो गया।
                                                                          
                                                                           

[Actual Hindi]: पटाखे की दुकान में आग से लोगों में हड़कंप मच गया।
==================================================

[English]: The fire brigade officer, Dani Ram, said the fire was brought under control in time. 
[Hindi]: आगदार अधिकारी डानी राम ने कहा कि आग समय में खाली कर दी गई। 
                                                                       
If you are facing any difficulty with any question or answer then please write us on our facebook page https://www.facebook.com/groups/546978364550335/   

[Actual Hindi]: दमकल अधिकारी दानी राम ने बताया कि समय रहते आग पर काबू पा लिया गया था।
==================================================

[English]: Following the incident the shopkeepers in the market have been sternly requested to take all necessary safety precautions. 
[Hindi]: अपराध के बाद शहर में विकास के लिए ख़ासी सुविधाओं का प्रारंभिक आवश्यकता है। 

Note: This problem will be updated once you submit your solution and we check it for correctness.
[Actual Hindi]: घटना को देखते हुए बाजार में भी दुकानदारों से सुरक्षा बरतने के सख्त निर्देश दे दिए गए हैं।
==================================================

[English]: Apart from the cinemas of South India, her films also make a big impact in the cinemas halls in Singapore and Malaysia. 
[Hindi]: अपार्ट से दक्षिण भारत के सिनेमा से परे हर एक इन्स्टिट्यूट की अपनी फ़िल्में भी बड़ी प्रभाव हैं।
[Actual Hindi]: दक्षिण भारत के अलावा सिंगापुर और मलेशिया के सिनेमाघरों में जिसकी फिल्म अक्सर धूम मचाती रहती है।
==================================================

[English]: The name of the actress is "Avni Modi". 
[Hindi]: अभिनेत्री का नाम "अवनी मोदी" है। 

[Actual Hindi]: इस एक्ट्रेस का नाम है "अवनि मोदी"।
==================================================

[English]: Avni is from the Gandhinagar district of Gujrat. 
[Hindi]: अवनी गांधीनगर जिले की आदित्य हैं।
                                                                                                           

*/
class Solution {
    public String translate(String s) {
        char[] ch = s.toCharArray();
        
        int i=0;
        int j=ch.length-1;
        
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        
        while (i<j){
            
            if (Character.isUpperCase(ch[i])){
                sb.append(' ');
                i++;
            }else{
                sb.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch[i]));
                i++;
            }
            
            if (Character.isUpperCase(ch[j])){
                sb.append(' ');
                j--;
            }else{
                sb.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch[j]));
                j--;
            }
            
        }
        
        return sb.toString();
    }
}
[Actual Hindi]: अवनि गुजरात के जिले गांधीनगर की रहने वाली हैं।
==================================================

[English]: Avni was interested in acting from childhood, but until college she wasn't able to brush up her acting skills. 
[Hindi]: अवनी ने आत्मा के अंदर अभिनेता की चाहत करने से पहले कृष्ण में काम करने का इंतजार कर रखा था।
[Actual Hindi]: अवनि को बचपन से ही एक्टिंग का शौक था, लेकिन कॉलेज तक वे एक्टिंग में अपने पैर नहीं जमा सकी थीं।
==================================================

[English]: Because of this, her college script writer even once told her to,"forget about acting, as you don't even understand the A in Acting". 
[Hindi]: इसलिए, उसके स्क्रिप्ट लेखक एक बार अपनी को बताया, "काम करने के लिए अपनी आकांक्षा भी भूल जाओ, क्योंकि आप आकांक्षा 'A' को समझ नहीं पातें"

[Actual Hindi]: इसके चलते एक बार तो कॉलेज के स्क्रिप्ट राइटर ने अवनि से यहां तक कह दिया था कि एक्टिंग की बात तो दूर, तुम्हें तो एक्टिंग का ए भी नहीं आता।
==================================================

[English]: She was lost in the crowd of her school and college, but now she is making Gujarat very famous in the Tamil Film Industry. 
[Hindi]: इस बच्ची के अपने स्कूल और कॉलेज में एक महाभारत में अपने पास लगा हुआ उन्हें टमिल फ़िल्म उद्योग में गुजरात को प्रसिद्ध बनाने की कोशिश कर रही हैं।

### 10. [Linguistic Requirements for the Language:](https://github.com/sid-kumar/Lexical-Similarity-Analysis/blob/master/Language%20Requirement.md)
The following are the linguistic requirements for the language. Please check your language if it meets all these requirements. If not, then you can still participate but your project might be rejected. 
1. 256 character limit for each word (inclusive of spaces).
2. No punctuation marks except spaces.
3. Words should start with a capital letter and end with a full stop.
4. Words must have a minimum of two characters.
5. Words should not contain numbers or special symbols like $, @ etc.
6. Words must be in lower case letters.
7. Words must not contain more than one space between them.
8. Each word must have exactly one meaning.
9. Word forms should be in their standard form (e.g., 'dogs' instead of 'dog').
10. Words must be written in alphabetical order.

### 11. [Data Requirements for the Language:](https://github.com/sid-kumar/Lexical-Similarity-Analysis/blob/master/Data%20Requirements.md)
The following are the data requirements for the language. Please check your language if it meets all these requirements. If not, then you can still participate but your project might be rejected. 
1. At least 500 words for training and testing.
2. At least 1000 sentences per document.
3. Sentences should be in English and translated into the target language.
4. The data should be split into training and test sets.
5. The dataset should include both the original and the translation versions of the documents.
6. Documents should be written in a clear and concise manner.
7. The data should be well-formatted and easy

==================================================

[Hindi]: समाज अपने आवश्यकताओं के लिए इस स्थल पर आकर आ गये।

[Hindi]: घर के आस-पास लोग अपनी मदद करके पुलिस पर ख़बर दी।

[Actual Hindi]: तत्काल आसपास के लोगों ने इसकी सूचना पुलिस को दी।
==================================================

[English]: Councillor Anup Sav arrived. 
[Hindi]: साहिरी अनुप सव आया।

[Actual Hindi]: पार्षद अनूप साव पहुंचे।
==================================================

[English]: Anjali had also arrived by that time. 
[Hindi]: एंजली अभी भी उतरी हुई थी।

*/

class Solution {
    public String translate(String s) {
        // Write your code here
        String[] arr = s.split(" ");
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        
        for (int i=0;i<arr.length-1;i++) {
            if (i == 0 || i == arr.length - 1){
                sb.append(arr[i]).append(" ");
            } else {
                sb.append(arr[i]).append(" के लिए ");
            }
            
            sb.append(arr[i+1]);
        }
        
        return sb.toString().trim();
    }
}

[Hindi]: इस लड़की को उसने एक भाई की बताया। 
and the second sentence is [Hindi] He asked me where I had been. 
[English]: वह मुझे अपने कहा कहा से मैं कहा कहा गया था। 
then your answer should be [Hindi]: वह मुझे कहा कहा से मैं ऐसा कहा कहा गया था।

###### Solution:
The following steps can be used for this problem:
* Read the input string carefully.
* Find out the position of 'in', which should come after 'the'.
* Find the position of 'of' which comes after 'the'.
* Count the number of words between 'in' and 'of'.
* Now find the next word after 'of'. This will be the first word in the sentence.
* Then count the number of words between the first word and 'and'.
* Finally count the number of words between 'and' and 'police'.

==================================================

[Hindi]: अगर कोई ग़लती हुई तो हम अकेले थे। 


[Actual Hindi]: यदि बच्ची कुछ कर लेती तो क्या होता।

[English]: The taxi driver was injured in the incidence. 
[Hindi]: टैक्सी चauffeur इस घटना में झगड़ गया।


"""

import argparse
import os
import sys
from typing import List

sys.path.append("../")

from translator_main import translate_english_to_hindi


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    parser.add_argument(
        "--input", type=str, default="data/example.txt", help="Input file path"
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--output", type=str, default="data/output.txt", help="Output file path"
    )
    args = parser.parse_args()

    if not os.path.isfile(args.input):
        print("Input file {} does not exist!".format(args.input))
        return -1

    sentences = []
    with open(args.input) as f:
        for line in f:
            sentences.append(line.strip())

    translated_sentences = translate_english_to_hindi(sentences)

    with open(args.output, "w+") as f:
        for i, sent in enumerate(translated_sentences):
            f.write(f"{i}. {sent}\n")

    print("Done!")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

##### 4. Hindi Grammar for Class X

The grammar portion is very easy to understand as it has only few rules which you need to follow. Here we have mentioned some important points regarding this topic. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X contains only few rules so its easier to remember. 
* There are many ways to write a word in hindi. 
* There are some rules regarding the usage of words like "Dhan" , "Ghar" etc. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X has only 5 parts of speech i.e. Nouns, Pronouns, Verbs, Adjectives and Adverbs. 
* There are some special rules for writing numbers in hindi like "Khata" , "Tola" etc. 
* Some words in hindi are used in plural form. 
* There are some special words in hindi which are used in both singular and plural forms. 
* Hindi Grammar for Class X also includes the use of punctuation marks.

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
import java.io.*;
class Test
{
    public static void main(String[] args)
    {
        //your code here
        Scanner sc=new Scanner(System.in);
        String str="";
        int i=0;
        System.out.println("Enter your text");
        str=sc.nextLine();
        for (i = 0; i < str.length(); i++)
        {
            if((str.charAt(i)>='a' && str.charAt(i)<='z')||(str.charAt(i)>='A' && str.charAt(i)<='Z'))
                System.out.print((char)(str.charAt(i)+32));
            else
                System.out.print((char)(str.charAt(i)));
        }
    }
}

### Part 3 - Difficulty Level: Easy

The following sentences have been taken from an interview with Narendra Modi on 14th September 2013. The interviewer asks questions in English and the answers are provided in Hindi. The interview has been translated into English for you to translate it back into Hindi. Please do not use any online translation tools or machine translations as they are unreliable.

#### Instructions

For each question, please provide your answer in Hindi using the format shown in Example 1.

User:                                   Interviewee:
Example 1:
[English]: Q: Why should people vote for you?
[Hindi]: जवाब: इसके लिए क्यों लोगों ने मैं वोट देना चाहिए?

Example 2:
[English]: Q: What are the top three issues facing Gujarat today?
[Hindi]: जवाब: गुजरात में ऐसे कौन सी तीन सब्जेक्ट हैं जिन्हें प्राप्त करना चाहिए?

Example 3:
[English]: Q: How would you define yourself?
[Hindi]: जवाब: मेरा कैसे अपना प्रतिभाओं का अनु
[Actual Hindi]: वहीं पर कभी यह कहकर सबको चौंका दिया कि जब तक उन्हें खुदाई स्थल पर नहीं बुलाया जाता तब तक सोना नहीं निकलने वाला है।
==================================================

[English]: When asked about the differences in his comments he became annoyed and started accusing the Government and the SSI, talking about what exactly is being done at the excavation site and that the media is being banned from entry there. 
[Hindi]: अपने टिप्पणियों के बीच अलग-अलग रूप से अपराध के खिलाफ आरोप लगाने के बाद वह झूठ बोलते हुए सरकार और सीएसआई को हमला करते हुए अन्तराल की इस खोल स्थल पर क्या है क्या हो रहा है और क्या वह मीडिया को इस खोल स्थल पर कुछ नहीं करना चाहते हैं?

[Actual Hindi]: बातों में लगातार आ रही भिन्नता पर सवाल होने पर सरकार ने बौखलाते हुए एएसआई और प्रशासन पर आरोप लगाने शुरू कर दिए और कहा कि ऐसा कौन सा काम खुदाई स्थल पर हो रहा है जो मीडिया को प्रतिबंधित किया जा रहा है।
==================================================

[English]: We had demanded a live telecast of the excavation. 
[Hindi]: हमने खोज के लिए आर्टिस्ट की सामग्री लाइव तेलिका चाहिए।

[Actual Hindi]: हमने तो खुदाई के सीधे प्रसारण की मांग की थी।
==================================================

[English]: However, he did agree that the SSI excavation team is digging on the right spot, as he had indicated. 
[Hindi]: हालांकि वह इस मार्ग पर खड़ा कर रहे हैं, जो उन्होंने अनुरागित कर दिया था।

[Actual Hindi]: उन्होंने यह जरूर माना कि उन्होंने जिस स्थान पर बताया गया था एएसआई की टीम वहीं पर खुदाई कर रही है।
==================================================

[English]: Meanwhile, after a day's rest the SSI team has started digging again today but could not make even a centimetre of progress. 
[Hindi]: आखिरकार अपने दिन का सोपा ख़ामोश होकर सीएसई टीम आज भी साइंग अपने काम में शुरू कर रही हैं लेकिन एक सेंटीमीटर की तक को बढ़ा नहीं सका।
[Actual Hindi]: बहरहाल, एक दिवसीय विश्राम के बाद एएसआई की टीम ने आज खुदाई का काम पुनः शुरू कर दिया पर एक सेंटीमीटर भी आगे नहीं बढ़ सकी।
==================================================

[English]: The Assistant District Collector, Vijay Shankar Dubey, said that today the SSI team kept cleaning the area excavated so far, 4.80 m., the whole day. 
[Hindi]: अन्य जिलाधिकारी विजय शंकर दुबे ने कहा कि आज सीएसआई टीम दो दिन तक ही सामान्य क्षेत्र के प्रति प्राप्त खोले क्षेत्र को सफाई करने के लिए बहुत से समय बिताया।
[Actual Hindi]: उपजिलाधिकारी विजय शंकर दुबे ने बताया कि आज दिनभर एएसआई की टीम अभी तक हुई पूरी खुदाई 4 मीटर 80 सेमी की सफाई करती रही है।
==================================================

[English]: If the Tata Workers Union is not able to provide any permanent solution to the Tata Steel Employees quarter extension issue, then the secretary-general would have to fix a date for a quick requisition meeting. 
[Hindi]: अगर टाटा का कार्यकर्ता संघ टाटा स्टील के कर्मचारियों के आवश्यक समस्या का परिणाम से एक परिणाम नहीं पाता है तो सचिवालय के प्रमुख जिनके समस्या का परिणाम के समय एक ही समय पर तलाक सम्मेलन की तारीख निर्धारित करना होगा।

**Input Format**
The first line contains an integer 'T' denoting the number of test cases. Then each of the next 'T' lines contain an English Sentence which has to be translated into Hindi.

**Constraints**
1 <= T <= 5
1 <= Length of English Sentence <= 40

**Output Format**
For each test case, print the translation of the sentence on a new line.

**Sample Input**
6
[English]: टाटा का कार्यकर्ता संघ टाटा स्टील के कर्मचारियों के आवश्यक समस्या का परिणाम से एक परिणाम नहीं पाता है तो सचिवालय के प्रमुख जिनके समस्या का परिणाम के समय एक ही समय पर तलाक सम्मेलन क
[Actual Hindi]: टाटा स्टील कर्मचारियों के क्वार्टर एक्सटेंशन के मुद्दे पर अगर टाटा वर्कर्स यूनियन कोई स्थाई समाधान नहीं दिला पा रही है तो महासचिव को जल्द से जल्द रिक्वीजिशन मीटिंग बुलाने की तिथि घोषित करनी चाहिए।
==================================================

[English]: If the decision on a grade revision is taking time, then efforts shall be made to provide these employees with some interim amount. 
[Hindi]: अगर एक अंक परिवर्तन की निर्णय का लेना समय आता है, तो इन व्यक्तियों को कुछ समय तक के रूप में कुछ सम्झदार खाता भी मिलेगी।
[Actual Hindi]: अगर ग्रेड रिवीजन समझौते में देरी हो रही है तो कर्मचारियों को अंतरिम राशि दिलाने की कोशिश की जानी चाहिए।
==================================================

[English]: With these two demands, around ten union members met the General Secretary B.K Dinda on Friday evening and put forward a proposal. 
[Hindi]: इन दो अभिव्यक्तियों के साथ दो दिन पहले अध्यक्ष बी.के. दिन्दा के साथ आरती करके दो मांगें एक समय पहले उन्हें प्रस्ताव पेश किया गया।
                                                                       

[Actual Hindi]: इन्हीं दो मांगों को लेकर शुक्रवार की शाम रिक्वीजिशन के लिए आवेदन देने वाले यूनियन के करीब दस कमेटी मेंबर महासचिव बीके डिंडा से मिले।
==================================================

[English]: While speaking, Dinda mentioned that on Friday the issue of the extension could not be discussed between the Management and the Union. 
[Hindi]: अपनी बात में दिन्दा ने कहा कि फ्रेडे की एक बार उन्हें संपर्क में संपर्क करने की ख़ास बात का विस्तार नहीं था।

[Actual Hindi]: बातचीत के दौरान डिंडा ने बताया कि एक्सटेंशन के मुद्दे पर शुक्रवार को प्रबंधन व यूनियन के बीच कोई वार्ता नहीं हो सकी है।
==================================================

[English]: An Office Bearer meeting would be held on Saturday, at which this issue would be discussed. 
[Hindi]: सोमवार को अध्यक्ष समिति का मुख्य सभा आयोजित होगा, जहां यह विषय वार्ता कराए जाएगा।

### Input Format
The input file will contain an english sentence along with its translation into hindi language.

### Output Format
The output should consist of one line for each input line containing the translation of the english sentence into hindi.

### Sample Input
```
[English]: The noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
[Hindi]: ध्वनि प्रदूषण 100 डेसीबल तक पहुँच गया।
```

### Sample Output
```
[Hindi]: ध्वनि प्रदूषण 100 डेसीबल तक पहुँच गया।
```

[Actual Hindi]: शनिवार को इस मुद्दे पर ऑफिस बियरर मीटिंग बुलाकर विचार-विमर्श किया जाएगा।
==================================================

[English]: Among the people who went to meet the General Secretary were Ghulam Moinuddin, Manjit Singh, Saroj Pandey, Mahendra Singh, Dharmendra Upadhyay, Lal Bahadur Upadhyay, Ravi Shankar Pandey, Munneshwar Pandey and Girish. 
[Hindi]: अन्तराष्ट्रीय कार्यकर्ता अर्पित से में आए लोगों में थे : ग़ुलाम मुनेदीन, मनजित सिंह, सरोज पांडेय, महेंद्र सिंह, धर्मेंद्र उपाध्याय, लाल बहादुर उपाध्याय, रवि शंकर पांडेय, मुन्नेश्वर पांडेय और गिरीश।

### Part B - Data Conversion:
This section will have questions based on conversion of data into various formats. For example, conversion of Decimal to Binary or vice versa, conversion of Roman Numerals to Arabic Numbers etc.

#### Example:
Converting Decimal to Binary

Input:    
64 = 100100
Output:   
100100

Input:    
158 = 1011101
Output:   
1011101

Input:    
397 = 1111111
Output:   
1111111

Input:    
-35 = 1001101
Output:   
1001101

Input:    
-27 = 1011100
Output:   
1011100

Input:    
128 = 1000000
Output:   
1000000

Input:    
255 = 1111111
Output:   
1111111

Input:    
158 = 1011101
Output:   
1011101

[Actual Hindi]: महासचिव से मिलने गए प्रतिनिधिमंडल में गुलाम मोइनुद्दीन, मंजीत सिंह, सरोज पांडे, महेन्द्र सिंह, धर्मेन्द्र उपाध्याय, लाल बहादुर उपाध्याय, रवि शंकर पांडेय, मुनेश्वर पांडेय व गिरीश शामिल रहे।
==================================================

[English]: The Corporate Services Deputy V.P. was in the city but could not meet the Union officers. 
[Hindi]: शहर में अधिकारियों के साथ स्थानांतरण करने के लिए सर्व सेवा विभाग के अधिकारी था।



[Actual Hindi]: डिप्टी वीपी कॉरपोरेट सर्विसेज शहर में मौजूद रहे लेकिन यूनियन पदाधिकारियों से बातचीत नहीं हो सकी।
==================================================

[English]: This issue would probably now be discussed on Monday. 
[Hindi]: इस समस्या अब आज से बाद में विवाद किया जा सकता है।

##### Input Format
First line contains T, number of test cases (T<=10). Then for each test case it has two lines. First line contains N, total number of sentences(N>=1) and second line contains N sentences.

Each sentence is made up of maximum 50 words. Each word can contain alphabets and digits from 'a' to 'z', 'A' to 'Z'.


##### Output Format
For each test case print one line containing output of translation of all the sentences given as input.

##### Sample Input
4
7
This issue would probably now be discussed on Monday.
Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains.
The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.

##### Sample Output
सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।
आज से बाद में विवाद किया जा सकता है।

So the answer should be "आज से बाद में विवाद किया जा सकता है"

In the second example we have to translate "Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains." into Hindi.

The correct answer is [D].

##### Question 563:

Which one of the following pairs does not have the same meaning?

(A): Cunning : Crafty (B): Lonely : Solitary (C): Deliberate : Careful (D): Pure : Innocent

##### Question 564:

Which one of the following sentences contains an error? If there is no error, select 'No Error'.

(A): I would like to see you in the morning.
(B): I would like to meet you tomorrow.
(C): I would like to speak with you next week.
(D): I would like to talk to you soon.

##### Question 565:

In which one of the following sentences has the verb used correctly?

(A): I have been looking for him everywhere.
(B): He had been waiting for her all day long.
(C): She had been waiting for me since morning.
(D): He had been searching for his car all night.

##### Question 566:

Which one of the following words can be substituted for the word 'thought' without changing its meaning?

(A): Idea (B): Thinking (C): Thoughts (D): Thoughtless

##### Question 567:

Which one of the following phrases or expressions means the same as the phrase 'at any time'?

(A): At any point of time (B): Anytime (C): Whenever (D): Whatever

##### Question 568:

What is the correct form of the verb given in bold in the sentence below?

(A): It was not easy for him to do so.
(B): It was not easy for him doing so.
(C): It was not easy for him to done so.
(D): It was not easy for him to do it.

##### Question 569:

Choose the word which is most nearly the SAME in meaning as the word printed in bold as used in the passage.
[Actual Hindi]: प्रकाश पर्व दिवाली आज से शुरू हो गई है।
==================================================

[English]: Dhanteras or Small Diwali is on Friday. 
[Hindi]: धनतेरस या छोटा दिवाली आज की रात है।
                                                                       
Translate the following Sentences into Hindi using English as source language and vice-versa.
Example 1:
[English]: A man who had been missing for two days was found dead yesterday evening.
[Hindi]: एक मानव जिसे दो दिनों में खो गया था हमेशा की रात में अब मृत हो गया था।
Example 2:
[English]: The police have arrested four people in connection with the murder of a businessman.
[Hindi]: पुलिस ने मुंबई के एक बिज़नेसमैन की हत्या के संबंध में चार लोगों को गिरफ्तार कर लिया है।

[Actual Hindi]: शुक्रवार को छोटी दिवाली यानी की धनतेरस है।
==================================================

[English]: As well as Diwali house decorations, beautiful rangolis are also an attraction. 
[Hindi]: आप अपने घर के पर्यटन के साथ दीवाली की खूबसूरत रंगलीयों भी भी खास हैं।

[Actual Hindi]: दिवाली में घरों की साज-सज्जा के साथ एक आकर्षण खूबसूरत रंगोलियां भी हैं।
==================================================

[English]: Beautiful rangolis in the front yards or courtyards of houses are making the houses more beautiful. 
[Hindi]: घरों के आगामी खाली हैं या ओर के ऊपर ढेर ही अच्छे होने के लिए बेहद खूबसूरत रंगली की परिकल्पना है।

[Actual Hindi]: घर के बाहर या आंगन में बनी खूबसूरत रंगोली घर की खूबसूरती में चार-चांद लगा देती है।
==================================================

[English]: We have chosen some pictures from Gujarat on this occasion. 
[Hindi]: इस अवसर पर गुजरात के एक तहख़ाने से चुने गए हैं किसी तस्वीरें।


[Actual Hindi]: इसी मौके पर हम ये कुछ तस्वीरें गुजरात से चुनकर लाए हैं।

[Actual Hindi]: बैठक में सांसद प्रतिनिधि प्रो. प्रवीण चौधरी ने कहा कि सहकारिता विभाग हरित क्रांति के लाभुकों को राशि दे ताकि किसान आगे बढ़ें।
==================================================

### 4. Sentence Rearrangement (Rearrange sentences in the order they were originally written)

Sentences are rearranged to form a meaningful paragraph. Each question has four sentences and one of the sentences has been omitted. Choose the answer which best completes the passage.

Example:

[English]: A. He is a very hardworking person.
B. He always tries his best to complete his work on time.
C. He also helps others whenever he can.
D. He is an excellent student.
E. His teachers like him very much.

Correct Answer: [A][B][C][D][E]

[Actual Hindi]: अमेरिका में राजनेताओं के नाम पर सरकारी योजनाएं नहीं चलाई जातीं।
==================================================

[English]: Their justification in India is pathetic. 
[Hindi]: इंडिया में अपने विरोधाभास का अर्थ बेकार है।

### Question-4:
The following question consists of two sentences which have errors and/or require rephrasing. Find out which part of the sentence has an error and select the appropriate option corresponding to the error. If there is no error, select No Error as your answer.

1. 
  I don't know what I will do next week. 
  
  
  (A) I don't know what I will do next week.
(B) I don't know what will I do next week.
(C) I don't know what am I going to do next week.
(D) I don't know what I am going to do next week.

2. 
  She asked me why she had not received my letter. 
  
  
  (A) She asked me why I hadn't received her letter.
(B) She asked me why she didn't receive my letter.
(C) She asked me why she didn't received my letter.
(D) She asked me why she didn't received my letters.

3. 
  I saw him standing near the door. 
  
  
  (A) I saw him standing near the door.
(B) I saw him standing by the door.
(C) I saw him standing at the door.
(D) I saw him standing for the door.

4. 
  He said that he was tired because he had been working hard all day. 
  
  
  (A) He said that he was tired because he had worked hard all day.
(B) He said that he was tired because he had been working hard all day.
(C) He said that he was tired because he had work hard all day.
(D) He said that he was tired because he had worked hard all day.

5. 
  The police were called when we found the body. 
  
  
  (A) The police were called when we found the body.
(B) The police were called after we found the body.
(C)

### Day 2: Sentence Translation

The goal for today is to translate sentences from Hindi to English and vice versa. The system will take your input as the source language (from which you have to translate) and output the translation into target language.

To do this, you need to install Python and the NLTK library on your computer.

Installation instructions can be found [here](https://github.com/NLP-Project/Translate).

Once you've installed it, download the dataset files by clicking on the "Download" button under the title "Training Set".

You can also find the files here: https://drive.google.com/open?id=1XZpG5n8mVrE3vBJRgj7zYfC4eWQPqD6k

Move these files to a folder called `data` in the project directory.

Next, create a file called `sentences.txt` with the following contents:

```
Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains.
The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
Names like Gandhi Nagar, Patel Airport, Ambedkarpuram or Vivekanandapuram add an historical inspiration.
```

Then run the program by opening up a terminal window and typing:

```bash
python train_translator.py data/sentences.txt
```

If everything went well, you
[Actual Hindi]: गांधी नगर, पटेल हवाई अड्डा, अंबेडकरपुरम या विवेकानंदपुरम जैसे अनेक नाम प्रेरक इतिहास से जोड़ते हैं।
==================================================

[English]: In a recent survey conducted just two to three months ago, it was shown that half of the country's villages and cities are associated with the name of Rama. 
[Hindi]: अंतर्गत अपनी आखिरी दो-तीन महीने में पाया जानकारी है कि देश के हल्दी और शहरों में राम के नाम से पांच घंटे की हिस्से हैं।
[Actual Hindi]: अभी दो-तीन माह पूर्व हुए एक सर्वेक्षण में देश के आधे से च्यादा गांव-नगर राम नाम से जुड़े बताए गए थे।
==================================================

[English]: Extra vigilance is required in naming the country, period, culture, civilisation and history. 
[Hindi]: अतिरिक्त निरीक्षण आवश्यक है इसे देश, वर्ष, संस्कृति, संस्कृति और इतिहास की नामावली करने के लिए।
[Actual Hindi]: नामकरण में देश, काल, संस्कृति, सभ्यता और इतिहास के प्रति अतिरिक्त सजगता की आवश्यकता होती है।

### Question-5 : 
What is the difference between 'a' and 'an'? When should you use 'a' and when should you use 'an'? 

#### Solution:
Ans: A and an both mean “one” but they are used differently in different situations.
* An is used before a word beginning with a vowel sound (a as in apple).
* A is used before a word beginning with a consonant sound (a as in apple) or a silent letter (a as in about).

Examples:
An apple is red.
A dog barks.
An hour ago I went to the park.
I am not sure if I want to go to the party.
The party will be held on Friday night.

#### Explanation:
This question tests your knowledge of the usage of articles like ‘a’ and ‘an’. 
You need to explain the difference between these two articles. 

### Question-6 : 
Which one of the following sentences contains a dangling modifier? If so, where does it occur? 

#### Solution:
Ans: The correct answer is option C.

#### Explanation:
This question tests your understanding of how to identify dangling modifiers. 
Dangling modifiers are phrases that do not refer to anything specific in the sentence. They can often cause confusion because they seem incomplete. 
In this case, the phrase “on a weekend afternoon” does not refer to any particular thing or person; instead, it describes the setting in

                pw.println(translate(words[0],words[1]));
            }else{
                pw.println(translate(words[0]));
            }
            
        }
        
    }

[Actual Hindi]: कन्नूर देश का ऐसा पहला जिला बन गया है, जिसमें अब कोई परिवार भूमिहीन नहीं है।
==================================================

[English]: The Central Rural development Minister Jairam Ramesh has declared that every poor family should have at least 3 cent. (approx. 120 square metres) of land to build a house. 
[Hindi]: केंद्रीय ग्रामीण विकास मंत्री जैरम रामेश ने कहा कि केवल सर्व गरीब परिवार को 3 सेंट की ख़ाली ही होनी चाहिए (अनुमान में 120 स्क्वायर मीटर) कि घर बना सकें।

###### Solution:
```python
import re

sentence = "The Central Rural development Minister Jairam Ramesh has declared that every poor family should have at least 3 cent. (approx. 120 square metres) of land to build a house."

sentence_translation = re.sub(r"([A-Za-z])", lambda x: x.group(1).lower(), sentence)

print(sentence_translation)
```

###### Output:
```
The central rural development minister jairam ramesh has declared that every poor family should have at least three cent. (approximately 120 square meters) of land to build a house.
```

[Hindi]: पुलिस की चीफ ने कहा कि ये अपराधियों एक बड़ा गैंग में हैं।


"""
import re
from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize
from nltk.stem.porter import PorterStemmer
from nltk.corpus import stopwords
import string

# Define the Porter Stemmer class
class PorterStemmer():
    def __init__(self):
        self._stemmer = PorterStemmer()
        
    # Get stemmed words using the Porter Stemmer class
    def get_stemmed_words(self, input_string):
        return [word for word in word_tokenize(input_string) if not word in string.punctuation]
    
    # Check whether the input string is an email or not
    def check_email(self, input_string):
        pattern = r'^[\w]+(\.\w+)+@[\w]+(\.\w+)+$'
        return re.match(pattern, input_string)

# Initialize the Porter Stemmer object
porter_stemmer = PorterStemmer()

# Read all lines from the file and store it in the list "lines"
with open('data/english-hindi.txt', 'r') as f:
    lines = f.read().split('\n')

# Iterate through each line and remove the stopwords from it
for i, line in enumerate(lines):
    cleaned_line = porter_stemmer.get_stemmed_words(line).lower()
    cleaned_line = ' '.join([word for word in cleaned_line if word not in stopwords.words('english')])
    print("{}: {}".format(i + 1, cleaned_line))

==================================================

The IEA’s World Energy Outlook 2019 projects that coal consumption will rise by 6%, even though the fuel has been hit hard by climate change concerns and falling costs for renewable power. Oil use will grow by 8%.
Coal use is expected to continue rising because it remains relatively cheap compared with other fossil fuels, especially natural gas, which will also see its use rise. Renewables such as solar and wind power will account for about half of all electricity generation by 2040.
The report predicts that carbon emissions will reach record levels in 2019, before plateauing through 2023. But emissions would still be well above pre-industrial levels in 2040.
“It is not too late to put the world onto a pathway consistent with limiting warming to 1.5 degrees Celsius,” said Fatih Birol, executive director of the IEA. “But we have no time to lose.”
In order to keep global temperatures within the 1.5 degree Celsius target set out under the Paris Agreement, the world needs to reduce emissions by nearly 7% every year until 2030. That would require a massive expansion of clean energy technologies, including wind and solar power, nuclear plants and carbon capture and storage technology, according to the report.

### Part - C: 
Now let's start the actual coding part.
First we will write the function for taking input and converting it into string. We will use Scanner class to take input from user and then convert it into String using StringBuffer class.
```java
public static void main(String[] args) {
    Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
    
    System.out.println("Enter the number of sentences you want to translate: ");
    int numSentences = sc.nextInt();
    System.out.println("\n");
    
    // Taking Input
    String strInput = "";
    for (int i=0; i<numSentences; i++) {
        strInput += "\nEnter the sentence no."+i+" : ";
        strInput += " ";
    }
    System.out.println(strInput);
    
    // Converting input into String
    StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
    for (int i=0; i<numSentences; i++) {
        sb.append("\n\t\t");
        sb.append("Enter the sentence no."+i+" : ");
        sb.append(" ");
    }
    String strInput = sb.toString();
}
```
Next we will define our main function where we will take the input from user and then call our translation function which we will implement later.
```java
// Main Function

    // Calling the translation function
    translateSentence();
}
```

### Part-3 : Sentence Correction 

Sentences have been taken from the Newspapers and magazines. The purpose of this part is to check your grammatical skills.

Example:

[English]: In the year 2019, the company earned a profit of Rs 50 crores, but in the year 2020 it has lost its profits by Rs 40 crores.
[Hindi]: 2019 में कंपनी ने आय 50 करोड़ रुपये कमाई हैं, लेकिन 2020 में आय 40 करोड़ रुपये से ज्यादा हार कर दिया हैं।

The correct translation of the above sentence should be:
[Hindi]: 2019 में कंपनी ने आय 50 करोड़ रुपये कमाई हैं, लेकिन 2020 में आय 40 करोड़ रुपये से ज्यादा हार कर दिया हैं।

The sentences which you will see in this section will be related to
[Actual Hindi]: पुलिस के मुताबिक बृहस्पतिवार देर रात 1 बजे पुलिस को सूचना मिला थी कि रोशन गार्डन इलाके में नाले के पास घायल अवस्था में युवक पड़ा है।
==================================================

- The output of each translation will consist of a single line containing a string of words separated by spaces.

10. [English]: He has also said that the vaccination drive will start as soon as possible.

==================================================

In this part we will analyse the data for the sentences which were translated incorrectly by the model. We will also discuss the challenges faced by our model and what improvements can be made to improve its performance.

#### Explanation for Sentence 1

The sentence in English was "Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains."

As you can see, the translation for the first word (Out) is incorrect. This is because the model did not recognize the word 'out' as it was not in the training set. As a result, the model generated an incorrect translation.

#### Explanation for Sentence 2

The sentence in English was "The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels."

As you can see, the translation for the second word (The) is incorrect. This is because the model did not recognize the word 'the' as it was not in the training set. As a result, the model generated an incorrect translation.

#### Explanation for Sentence 3

The sentence in English was "Similarly, in addition to the price of brass, copper utensil have also become more expensive."

As you can see, the translation for the third word (Similarly) is incorrect. This is because the model did not recognize the word 'similarly' as it was not in the training set. As a result, the model generated an incorrect translation.

#### Explanation for Sentence 4

The sentence in English was "In addition to the price of brass, copper utensils have also become more expensive."

from collections import Counter
import re
import string

def translate(english_sentence):
    # print("Before Translation")
    words = [word for word in english_sentence if word not in ['of', 'the']]
    print("After Removing Stopwords", len(words))
    
    words = [word for word in words if word not in ["is", "was"]]
    print("After Removing Stopwords and Verbs", len(words))

    # split the sentences into sentences and then remove stopwords
    sentences = [sentence.split() for sentence in english_sentence.split(".")]
    sentences = [sentence for sentence in sentences if sentence != []]
    print("After removing Stopwords", len(sentences))
    
    sentences = [sentence for sentence in sentences if sentence != []]
    print("After removing stopwords", len(sentences))
    
    # now convert all these sentences to lower case
    sentences = [sentence.lower() for sentence in sentences]
    print("After converting to Lower Case", len(sentences))

    # now replace the stopwords with empty strings
    sentences = [re.sub('([a-z])([A-Z])', r'\1 \2', sentence) for sentence in sentences]
    print("After Replacing Stopwords with Empty Strings", len(sentences))

    # now replace the stopwords with their respective hindi equivalents
    sentences = [re.sub('([a-z])([A-Z])', r'_\1_\2', sentence) for sentence in sentences]
